\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em These values encode the bit positions of the decode position. These values can be used to read the value of a flag bit by combining the base\+\_\+mode variable with AND with the flag position value. The result will be either 0 or 1, depending on if the flag is set or not. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\#define \mbox{\hyperlink{common_8h_a073ec1e277b3d058a124e241c473d5ee}{HAVE\+\_\+\+ENUM\+\_\+\+MAV\+\_\+\+CMD}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Commands to be executed by the MAV. They can be executed on user request, or as part of a mission script. If the action is used in a mission, the parameter mapping to the waypoint/mission message is as follows\+: Param 1, Param 2, Param 3, Param 4, X\+: Param 5, Y\+:Param 6, Z\+:Param 7. This command list is similar what ARINC 424 is for commercial aircraft\+: A data format how to interpret waypoint/mission data. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define HAVE\+\_\+\+ENUM\+\_\+\+MAV\+\_\+\+CMD}



Commands to be executed by the MAV. They can be executed on user request, or as part of a mission script. If the action is used in a mission, the parameter mapping to the waypoint/mission message is as follows\+: Param 1, Param 2, Param 3, Param 4, X\+: Param 5, Y\+:Param 6, Z\+:Param 7. This command list is similar what ARINC 424 is for commercial aircraft\+: A data format how to interpret waypoint/mission data.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define HAVE\+\_\+\+ENUM\+\_\+\+MAV\+\_\+\+MODE}



These defines are predefined OR-\/combined mode flags. There is no need to use values from this enum, but it simplifies the use of the mode flags. Note that manual input is enabled in all modes as a safety override.

These values encode the bit positions of the decode position. These values can be used to read the value of a flag bit by combining the base\+\_\+mode variable with AND with the flag position value. The result will be either 0 or 1, depending on if the flag is set or not.
